Tweak::Shunt(No Amp)::
  port_ =                0x48; // I2C port used by Acafruit_ADS1015
  bare_ =                   0; // If ADS to be ignored
  *cp_ibatt_bias_ =     0.000; // Global bias, A
  v2a_s_ =            -1189.30; // Selected shunt conversion gain, A/V
  vshunt_int_ =           0; // Sensed shunt voltage, count
  ishunt_cal_ =         0.000; // Sensed, calibrated ADC, A
Shunt(No Amp)::Tweak(No Amp)::
  max_change_ =               0.004; // Maximum allowed change to calibration scalar see 'N/MC'
  max_tweak_ =                0.040; // Maximum allowed calibration scalar see 'N/Mx'
  rp_delta_q_cinf_ =           41.4; // Charge infinity at past update see 'N/Mi', Coulombs
  rp_delta_q_dinf_ =            0.0; // Discharge infinity at past update see 'N/Mi', Coulombs
  sat_ =                          1; // Indication that battery is saturated, T=saturated
  delta_hrs_ =             0.011599; // Time since last allowed saturation see 'N/Mz', hr
  time_to_wait =           0.000000; // Time to wait before allowing saturation see 'N/Mw', hr
  tweak_sclr =                0.992; // Scalar on Coulombic Efficiency 'N/Mk'
  coul_eff_ =      0.99850;  // Coulombic Efficiency
